<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><b>Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><i>&#160;</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><i>Total Shares and Debt Principal Outstanding</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The Company will disclose on its website that
the Company currently has 31,389,589 total shares outstanding. The Company will also disclose on its website that the Company will have
approximately $140.3 million of outstanding debt principal as of September 30, 2025.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><i>Warrant Distribution FAQ</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On November 12, 2025, the Company made available
a document containing questions and answers (the &#8220;FAQ&#8221;) regarding the previously announced warrant distribution. The FAQ is
attached as Exhibit 99.4 to this Form 8-K, and supersedes in its entirety the FAQ previously made available by the Company on October
21, 2025.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The information furnished in this Current Report
under Item 7.01, including Exhibits 99.1, 99.2, 99.3 and 99.4, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise be subject to the liabilities of that Section,
nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;),
or the Exchange Act, except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><b>No Offer or Solicitation.</b> This communication
shall not constitute an offer to sell or the solicitation of an offer to buy any securities, nor shall there be any sale of these securities
in any state or jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under
the securities laws of any such state or jurisdiction.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The issuance of the Warrants in the Warrant Distribution
has not been registered under the Securities Act, as the distribution of a Warrant for no consideration does not constitute a sale of
a security under Section 2(a)(3) of the Securities Act. A Form 8-A registration statement and registration statement containing a prospectus
or prospectus supplement describing the terms of the Warrants have been filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;)
and are available on the SEC&#8217;s website located at http://www.sec.gov. Holders of Common Stock, the Company&#8217;s 5.50% Convertible
Senior Notes due 2030, the Company&#8217;s 2.5% Convertible Notes due 2030 and the Company&#8217;s currently outstanding warrants should
read the prospectus or prospectus supplement carefully, including the Risk Factors section included and incorporated by reference therein.
This communication contains a general summary of the Warrants. Please read the warrant agreement relating to the Warrants as it contains
important information about the terms of the Warrants.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE, DATED NOVEMBER 12, 2025
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">November 12, 2025</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B><I>DeFi Development Corp. Reports Strong Third
Quarter 2025 Earnings<BR></I>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>BOCA RATON, FL &mdash; November 12, 2025 &mdash;
DeFi Development Corp. (Nasdaq: DFDV)</B> (the &ldquo;Company&rdquo; or &ldquo;DeFi Dev Corp.&rdquo;), the first US public company with
a treasury strategy built to accumulate and compound Solana (&ldquo;SOL&rdquo;), today released its 3Q 2025 Shareholder Letter and Business
Update.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">To read the full update, please visit: <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">https://defidevcorp.com/investor?tab=earnings</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">A video update featuring CEO Joseph Onorati, CFO
John Han, COO &amp; CIO Parker White, and CSO Dan Kang will be uploaded to youtube.com/@DeFiDevCorp tomorrow, November 13, 2025, at approximately
8:00 a.m. Eastern Time. Management will address strategic highlights and take questions submitted in advance by both retail investors
and sell-side analysts.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">For more information, visit defidevcorp.com. To
stay up-to-date with the latest developments and insights, subscribe to our blog.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>About DeFi Development
Corp.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B></B></FONT>DeFi Development Corp. (Nasdaq: DFDV) has adopted a treasury policy under which the principal holding in its treasury
reserve is allocated to SOL. Through this strategy, the Company provides investors with direct economic exposure to SOL, while also actively
participating in the growth of the Solana ecosystem. In addition to holding and staking SOL, DeFi Development Corp. operates its own
validator infrastructure, generating staking rewards and fees from delegated stake. The Company is also engaged across decentralized
finance (DeFi) opportunities and continues to explore innovative ways to support and benefit from Solana&rsquo;s expanding application
layer.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The Company is an AI-powered online platform that
connects the commercial real estate industry by providing data and software subscriptions, as well as value-add services, to multifamily
and commercial property professionals, as the Company connects the increasingly complex ecosystem that stakeholders have to manage.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The Company currently serves more than one million
web users annually, including multifamily and commercial property owners and developers applying for billions of dollars of debt financing
per year, professional service providers, and thousands of multifamily and commercial property lenders, including more than 10% of the
banks in America, credit unions, real estate investment trusts (&ldquo;REITs&rdquo;), debt funds, Fannie Mae&reg; and Freddie Mac&reg;
multifamily lenders, FHA multifamily lenders, commercial mortgage-backed securities (&ldquo;CMBS&rdquo;) lenders, Small Business Administration
(&ldquo;SBA&rdquo;) lenders, and more. The Company&rsquo;s data and software offerings are generally offered on a subscription basis as
software as a service (&ldquo;SaaS&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Investor Contact:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">ir@defidevcorp.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Media Contact:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Prosek Partners</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">pro-ddc@prosek.com</P>

<DESCRIPTION>EXPLANATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES, DATED NOVEMBER 12, 2025
<TEXT>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.2</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Exhibit 99.2 - Explanation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">This Exhibit 99.2 to the accompanying Current
Report on Form 8-K of DeFi Development Corp. (&ldquo;we,&rdquo; &ldquo;us,&rdquo; or &ldquo;our&rdquo;) provides a discussion of the reasons
we believe that the inclusion of certain non-GAAP financial measures, as presented in the earnings press release furnished as Exhibit
99.1 to this Form 8-K, offers useful supplemental information to investors regarding our operating performance. Where applicable, this
Exhibit also describes any additional purposes for which management utilizes these non-GAAP financial measures.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Reconciliations between each non-GAAP financial
measure and the most directly comparable financial measure calculated in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the
United States (&ldquo;GAAP&rdquo;) are provided within the earnings press release itself. Non-GAAP financial information should be viewed
as a supplement to, and not as a substitute for, the comparable GAAP measures such as operating income, net income, earnings per share,
net cash provided by operating activities, or other performance and liquidity metrics prepared in accordance with GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><U>Adjusted Net Income (Loss) and Adjusted Earnings
per Share (&ldquo;EPS&rdquo;)</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Adjusted net income (loss) and adjusted EPS are
non-GAAP financial measures that management believes are useful to investors in evaluating period-over-period comparability and the results
of our ongoing operations. Adjusted net income (loss) and adjusted EPS are defined as net income (loss) including the impact of interest
expense associated with convertible notes and diluted earnings per common share, respectively, adjusted to exclude the impact of certain
events, loss on dispositions, or other charges that affect period-over-period comparability.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<DESCRIPTION>SEPTEMBER 2025 SHAREHOLDER LETTER AND BUSINESS UPDATE, DATED NOVEMBER 12, 2025
<TEXT>

</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.3</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Fellow shareholders,</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Optimizing Solana&rsquo;s native
yield is one of our key strengths, and this quarter proved it. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">In Q3
we delivered an average organic yield (AOY) o</FONT>f 11.4%<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>1</SUP></FONT>,
exce<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">eding our 10% guidance level, and higher than the yield offered by Coinbase (4.2%)<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>2</SUP></FONT>,
or BSOL ETF (7.0%)<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>3</SUP></FONT>, and higher than any
other digital asset treasury company (&ldquo;DAT&rdquo;). Our net income for the quarter was approximately $56M, and adjusted net
income was approximately $59.0M.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">For a DAT, organic yield is not
a side benefit. It is the engine of crypto accumulation. Every point of additional yield compounds directly into faster SOL-per-Share
(&ldquo;SPS&rdquo;) growth. With double-digit organic yield, our treasury effectively self-expands, generating SOL around the clock without
relying solely on new capital. The result is a structurally higher rate of crypto accumulation: one that outpaces passive vehicles and
continues compounding after every fundraise. This is the difference between a DAT that simply holds SOL and one that continuously generates
more of it. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Since our last shareholder update,
we grew our S</FONT>PS by 13% Q/Q to 0.0700,<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>4</SUP></FONT>
with to<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">tal SOL and SOL Equivalents<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>5</SUP></FONT>
of 2.2M and total shares outstanding of 31.4M. Our mission remains unchanged: grow SPS as quickly as possible for our shareholders. SPS
growth continues to be our North Star and is the clearest measure of execution for any DAT&rsquo;s performance.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Despite strong operational performance,
DFDV wasn&rsquo;t immune to the dynamic that challenged every DAT in Q3: broad-based mNAV compression as investor attention splintered
across hundreds of new entrants. This compression has been the main driver of our stock performance, with fully diluted mNAV declining
41%, from 1.4x at the time of our last earnings update to 0.8x today. That move accounts for nearly all of our 45% stock price decline
over the same period. Importantly, this trend was not unique to DFDV. For example, since July 16, the date MSTR reached its all-time high,
Strategy&rsquo;s mNAV fell by approximately 41% while its common equity declined 49%. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">We&rsquo;ve consistently said
that mNAV reflects the market&rsquo;s belief in a DAT&rsquo;s ability to accumulate more crypto. The broad-based decline suggests investors
are recalibrating expectations about how quickly DATs can compound as more players chase the same pool of capital. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">This is exactly why we built
DFDV differently from day 1. Unlike most DATs, our growth does not depend solely on recursive capital raises. Our SOL treasury generates
approximately 10% AOY, making it an accumulation engine that never sleeps</FONT>. This engine generates revenue and cash flow that help
us meet our operating and interest expenses. Our 10<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">% yield is unmatched among DATs and reflects
both our crypto expertise and Solana&rsquo;s deep onchain opportunity set. With more than 15% of our treasury now deployed onchain, we
expect our AOY to remain at 10% for the foreseeable future.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Despite the near-term mNAV pressure,
our conviction in Solana remains strong. Solana&rsquo;s key metrics - DAUs, transactions, revenues - all grew rapidly y/y in Q3. Our recently
disclosed $10,000 SOL/USD price target assumes Solana captures 7.5% market share of global value transfer<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>6</SUP></FONT>
in the years ahead. Even in a scenario where Solana captures 1% of all global value transfer, we estimate SOL would reach approximately
$1,300. This would bring the value of our treasury to $2.6B vs. $344M today.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">It&rsquo;s still early. Our team
remains energized by the opportunity to define what it means to be a best-in-class DAT. As we continue to build the bridge between TradFi
and DeFi, our goal is to deliver value for shareholders through every phase of the crypto market cycle.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">This letter provides an overview of our Q3 2025 financials, a review
of our key initiatives such as our Treasury Accelerator, and a broader update on our business.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Thank you for your continued trust.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">In Service of SPS Growth,</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Joseph Onorati</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Putting Our Treasury to Work Onchain</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">As of this writing, more than
15% of our SOL treasury is deployed onchain across Solana DeFi, up from our last disclosure of approximately 10%. Expanding this footprint
allows us to optimize organic yield and capture opportunities unique to Solana&rsquo;s DeFi ecosystem.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">For example, in Q3 we executed
a looped staking strategy that generated over 100 bps of incremental net interest margin (NIM) on the capital allocated to it. Using dfdvSOL,
our liquid-staking token issued by Sanctum, as collateral on Kamino, we borrowed SOL and restaked it to our own validator. This allowed
us to capture additional yield and, because both the collateral and the borrow were SOL-denominated, this strategy carried no exposure
to liquidation risk from SOL price volatility. This is one of many ways our team engineers yield innovation without compromising balance
sheet safety.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Deploying capital across Solana
DeFi also strengthens the broader network and compounds our own long-term value. The success of DFDV is inseparable from the success of
Solana. The more robust and liquid the ecosystem becomes, the greater the opportunity for sustainable yield and SPS growth. With total
non-stablecoin TVL on Solana exceeding $10 billion<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>7</SUP></FONT>
and leading protocols like Jupiter and Kamino exceeding $3 billion eac</FONT>h, our $344 milli<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">on
treasury positions us as a meaningful liquidity provider across multiple verticals. This scale allows us to earn attractive returns while
directly supporting the Solana network.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"><B>The Treasury Accelerator Takes Flight </B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">This quarter, DFDV announced
three regional franchises through our Treasury Accelerator (TA) program: DFDV UK, DFDV Korea, and DFDV Japan. The goal of the TA is to
enable world-class teams to launch Solana DATs in markets where high investor appetite for crypto, limited institutional access, and local
tax dynamics create compelling opportunities for mNAV accretion. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">For DFDV, the model extends our
reach, broadens global demand for SOL, and introduces a new lever for NAV growth. We will retain equity stakes in each franchise and,
in some cases, asset management agreements. The TA program is designed to be both NAV and revenue accretive in both the near and long
term. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Each franchise is currently in
fundraising mode, and we will provide updates as they begin trading. Our long-term goal is to build a global network of DFDV-branded DATs.
Each franchise will compound SPS while reinforcing the broader Solana ecosystem and driving shareholder value back to DFDV.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Solana Ecosystem Update</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Q3 marked another breakout quarter for Solana, with surging network
activity, deeper liquidity, and accelerating adoption across DeFi, Real World Assets (RWAs), and consumer apps:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Key Solana Developments</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">&#9679;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B>DeFi &amp; Onchain Liquidity Expansio</B>n: In September, Solana DeFi TVL hit an all-time high of $13B, surpassing the previous
4Q&rsquo;21 peak. Growth was driven by deeper liquidity, renewed institutional participation, and demand for Solana-native yield products.<BR>
<BR>
</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

RWA issuance on the network. Platforms like Splyce and Chintai also expanded their tokenized securities infrastructure, reinforcing Solana&rsquo;s
leadership in the RWA sector.<BR>
<BR>
</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

Additionally, Moody&rsquo;s introduced onchain credit ratings using Solana infrastructure. DAT holdings of SOL grew from 0.3% to 2.3%
of total supply, underscoring SOL&rsquo;s credibility as a treasury-grade asset.<BR>
<BR>
</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

demonstrating the chain&rsquo;s speed and efficiency for sovereign payments and settlement.<BR>
<BR>
</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

throughput. The upcoming Alpenglow upgrade cleared governance review, paving the way for improved fee markets and validator efficiency.
A 100,000 TPS stress test validated Solana&rsquo;s unmatched performance potential.<BR>
<BR>
</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

for millions of users, while MetaMask, the largest Ethereum wallet, added .SOL domain support for Solana transactions. 1inch Wallet, another
Ethereum-native platform, launched full Solana compatibility, deepening cross-ecosystem connectivity.<BR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Q3 2025 Financials*</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Total revenue for the quarter was $4.6M, up 648% y/y. Of this, $3.8M was recognized as Digital Asset Treasury Revenue under U.S. GAAP,
representing income from staking and validator operations.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0">It is important to note this figure does <B>not</B> include revenue
generated from DeFi positions, which are generally realized as capital gains under accounting standards due to the structure of liquid
staking tokens (LSTs) and other yield-bearing assets. <B>As a result, our reported Digital Asset Treasury Revenue understates the total
economic yield generated by our treasury during the quarter. </B>We have updated the definition of Average Organic Yield accordingly (see
Appendix).</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Our diluted net income was approximately
$58M, resulting in a diluted earnings-per-share (&ldquo;EPS&rdquo;) of $1.83 for Q3 2025, and
approximately $59.0M on an adjusted basis, resulting in an adjusted EPS of $1.88, up from a $0.05 loss in Q3 of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">As of the date of this letter, we currently
have approximately 31.4 million common shares outstanding. Other financial data for the quarter will be reported in our upcoming
Form 10-Q, which we expect to file on or before November 19th.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Annualized Organic Yield</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Our annualized organic yield (AOY) for Q3
2025 was 11.4%</B>, or roughly 140 bps above our 10% target for the fiscal year. We expect AOY to average around 10% for the remainder
of the year, though actual results will fluctuate with staking dynamics, validator competition, and on-chain activity.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0">At our current SOL balance of 2.2 million SOL and a SOL/USD price of
$156, this equates to approximately ~$94k per day in SOL-denominated yield.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Marketing and Awareness </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">In Q3 and early Q4, DFDV meaningfully expanded awareness of both Solana
and our Digital Asset Treasury (DAT) model across institutional and retail audiences. From ringing the Nasdaq closing bell to hosting
the first Solana Investor Day, this was our strongest quarter yet for brand visibility, investor education, and ecosystem engagement.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">In August, we took center stage on Wall Street, ringing the Nasdaq
closing bell alongside the Solana Foundation and partners including BONK, WIF, Drift, Solflare, Fragmetric, Marinade, and Crypto.com.
Our Times Square tower campaign, &ldquo;<I>The Future of the Internet is Solana,</I>&rdquo; introduced DFDV to millions of investors and
cemented our status as the first Solana-native public company in U.S. markets.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">We also launched <B>SOLID: Solana Investor Day</B>, a first-of-its-kind
event connecting institutional investors with Solana&rsquo;s core teams including Jito, Sanctum, Marinade, Fragmetric, and Exchange.art.
The event served as a crash course on Solana, covering key metrics and real world use cases, and also highlighted DFDV&rsquo;s role as
the bridge between TradFi and DeFi.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Our leadership team carried that message globally. DFDV was featured
by CNBC, Bloomberg, CoinDesk, The Block, Fortune Crypto, The Defiant, Cointelegraph, and Seeking Alpha, with coverage highlighting our
Solana accumulation strategy and role in defining the DAT category. We took the stage at SuperTokyo 2025, Korea Blockchain Week, Token
2049, Pantera Blockchain Summit, and Solana Oriental, where we shared our &ldquo;<I>SOL to $10K</I>&rdquo; thesis, presented on mNAV dynamics,
and discussed the future of tokenized treasuries. We also appeared on Nasdaq TradeTalks, Solana Live with ThreadGuy, and P2P.org&rsquo;s
Digital Asset Treasury panel, reaching tens of thousands of investors worldwide. Together, these appearances reinforced DFDV as a leading
voice in defining how public companies can operate onchain and leverage Solana&rsquo;s performance edge.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Across digital channels, we scaled our content engine to drive investor
education and community alignment. Our Beehiiv blog reached record readership through reports such as &ldquo;<I>Digital Asset Treasuries:
The Next Frontier of Crypto Exposur</I>e&rdquo; and &ldquo;<I>The Next Best Crypto Trade? Solana DATs</I>,&rdquo; offering data-driven
insights into Solana&rsquo;s dominance and the mechanics of SPS and mNAV. Monthly business updates, our &ldquo;SOL to $10K&rdquo; presentation,
and growing YouTube coverage deepened transparency for shareholders. The <B>DFDV Degens</B> community grew rapidly across X and Reddit,
fostering direct, real-time dialogue between investors and the Solana ecosystem..</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Q3 was a defining period for DFDV&rsquo;s presence across capital markets,
digital communities, and mainstream media. We built meaningful momentum around our Solana-first mission, positioned DFDV as the face of
onchain treasury innovation, and set the stage for broader awareness and investor engagement heading into 2026.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Capital Raises</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Equity PIPE: </B>In August 2025, we closed a $125 million PIPE with
Cantor Fitzgerald at $12.50 per share. The net proceeds were deployed into spot SOL and discounted locked SOL positions, expanding treasury
holdings at favorable prices and increased overall NAV per share.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Preferred Equity (Registered Offering): </B>We recently announced
our intent to offer up to $65M of 10.0% Series C Cumulative Perpetual Preferred Stock. We have applied to list our Series C Preferred
Stock on the Nasdaq under the symbol &ldquo;CHAD.&rdquo; Preferred equity fits DFDV&rsquo;s structure uniquely well. While BTC DATs must
issue new common shares to service fixed coupons, our onchain yield engine that generates 10% AOY helps support sustainable, non-dilutive
preferred distributions.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>ELOC Usage</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0">To date, DFDV has raised approximately $58.2 million in net proceeds
via our Equity Line of Credit (ELOC), issuing roughly 2.9 million shares. We&rsquo;ve drawn only 1% of the $5 billion facility, leaving
$4.9 billion in remaining capacity for opportunistic deployment when trading at a premium to NAV.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>The Road Ahead </B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">As we head into the final weeks of 2025, our priorities are clear:
optimizing yield, leaning into our Treasury Accelerator, raising capital, and continuing to tell Solana&rsquo;s story.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">But our goals expand well beyond our near-term priorities. DFDV is
proving that a publicly listed company can move with crypto&rsquo;s speed and stay aligned with the community it serves. We&rsquo;re here
to build the bridge between TradFi and DeFi: to experiment boldly, to push boundaries, and to show that transparency and innovation can
coexist in public markets.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">We move quickly and embrace volatility. The market may fluctuate, but
our conviction won&rsquo;t.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">In Service of SPS growth,</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The DFDV Team</P>

tomorrow, November 13, 2025. CFO John Han, COO &amp; CIO Parker White, and CSO Dan Kang will all be on the video to answer questions submitted
by sellside analysts and retail investors.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 8; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->8<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Appendix</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B><I>Annualized Organic Yield </I></B><I>is a
key performance indicator (&ldquo;KPI&rdquo;) used by management to evaluate staking performance across our treasury assets. It is calculated
as:</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B><I>(Total SOL Generated / Average Stake and
Onchain SOL Balance) &times; 4</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>This metric reflects annualized, SOL-denominated
returns based on total yield generated from both staking operations and onchain DeFi positions, including liquid staking tokens (LSTs)
and other protocol-based activities. Because certain DeFi returns are recognized as capital gains rather than revenue under GAAP, AOY
serves as a broader economic measure of organic yield than &ldquo;Digital Asset Treasury Revenue.&rdquo;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>This KPI is unaudited and presented to provide
transparency into how management measures and optimizes onchain yield generation. Results may vary quarter to quarter based on staking
dynamics, validator performance, market conditions, and onchain activity. Past performance is not indicative of future results.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B><I>Average Stake and Onchain SOL Balance</I></B><I>
represents the arithmetic average of total SOL actively deployed across staking and DeFi strategies during the reporting period. This
includes SOL staked to validators operated by, or in partnership with, DeFi Development Corp., as well as SOL utilized in yield-generating
onchain positions such as liquid staking tokens (LSTs), lending, or liquidity provision.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>This figure reflects the effective capital
base generating organic yield and serves as the denominator in the calculation of Annualized Organic Yield (AOY).</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B><I>mNAV</I></B><I> is a KPI that measures our market capitalization
as a multiple of our underlying Net Asset Value. It is calculated as: </I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B><I>Market Capitalization / Net Asset Value</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>We present mNAV across four views:</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><I>1.</I></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B><I>Market Capitalization / SOL</I></B><I>: Basic measure. Market cap divided by the market value of SOL holdings.</I></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"><I>2.</I></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B><I>Equity / (SOL &ndash; Debt)</I></B><I>: Adjusts NAV by subtracting outstanding debt (convertible notes, SOL-denominated loans).</I></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"><I>3.</I></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B><I>Equity / (SOL &ndash; Debt): </I></B><I>Pro Forma for In-The-Money Convertible Debt Conversion. Assumes all convertible debt
converts to equity, removing the debt from NAV and incorporating the associated share dilution. Shares outstanding also includes RSUs
and vested stock options</I></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify; width: 0.25in"><I>4.</I></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B><I>Fully Diluted mNAV</I></B><I>: Assumes all convertible debt and in-the-money warrants convert to equity, removing the debt from
NAV and incorporating full dilution from both instruments.</I></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B><I>Market Capitalization</I></B><I> = shares outstanding &times;
current share price (adjusted for dilution where applicable).</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B><I>NAV</I></B><I> = total value of SOL holdings (and other liquid
assets) minus liabilities, marked to market.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">DeFi Development Corp. | 3Q&rsquo;25 | Shareholder Letter</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit 99.4</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>DeFi Development Corp. Stockholder FAQ
&ndash; Warrant Dividend Distribution</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B><I>Updated November 12, 2025</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>What is a warrant?</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">A warrant is an option to buy shares of common
shares issued directly by a company. It gives the holder the right, but not the obligation, to purchase a share of common stock at a specified
&ldquo;exercise price&rdquo;, on or before the warrant&rsquo;s &ldquo;expiration date.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>What is a warrant dividend?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">A warrant dividend is a distribution of warrants
by the company pro-rata to all existing common stockholders. As with a cash dividend, stockholders do not need to pay any amount or take
any other action to receive the distribution. In the case of a warrant dividend the value being distributed to all stockholders is in
the form of a warrant instead of cash.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Who will receive the warrants?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Holders of DFDV common stock as of the record
date of October 23, 2025 (&ldquo;stockholders&rdquo;) received one (1) warrant for each ten (10) shares of common stock held as of the
record date, rounded down to the nearest whole number.&nbsp;As an example, a stockholder who owns 320 or 327 shares of common stock would
receive 32 warrants. No fractional warrants were issued.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Holders as of the record date of the company&rsquo;s
pre-funded warrants issued on August 28, 2025, also received (1) warrant for each ten (10) shares of common stock underlying their pre-funded
warrants, rounded down to the nearest whole number, in accordance with the terms of the pre-funded warrants. No fractional warrants were
issued.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Holders of the company&rsquo;s 5.50% Convertible
Senior Notes due 2030 as of the record date (&ldquo;144A noteholders&rdquo;) also received warrants on an as-converted pass-through basis
in accordance with the terms of the governing indenture. 144A noteholders of each $1,000 principal amount received 4.32694 warrants, rounded
down to the nearest whole number for any fractional warrant. No fractional warrants were be issued. Given this pass-through, the warrant
distribution did not trigger a further adjustment to the conversion rate for the convertible notes.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Holders as of the record date of the company&rsquo;s
2.5% Convertible Notes due 2030 (&ldquo;PIPE noteholders&rdquo;) also received warrants on an as-converted pass-through basis. PIPE noteholders
of each $1,000 principal amount received 10.2669 warrants, rounded down to the nearest whole number for any fractional warrant. No fractional
warrants were issued.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>When is the expiration date?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">January 21, 2028, unless the Alternate Expiration
Price Condition is met.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>What is the Alternate Expiration Price
Condition?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">If, during any 30 consecutive trading days,
the volume weighted average price (VWAP) of DFDV common stock is at or above $27.00 for at least 20 of those days (not necessarily consecutive),
then the warrants will expire early &ndash; specifically at 5:00 p.m. New York City time on the business day immediately following the
20<SUP>th</SUP> such day or such other date as the Company may elect in accordance with the warrant agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">DFDV will issue a press release if the Alternate
Expiration Price Condition is triggered.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>What is the exercise price?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">$22.50 per share.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Why is DFDV issuing these warrants?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">DFDV believes that a warrant dividend distribution
is a stockholder-aligned approach to raising additional equity capital that rewards current stockholders and noteholders.&nbsp; It allows
existing DFDV investors to maintain their proportional ownership and participate equally in the company&rsquo;s future upside, or to monetize
their rights by selling the warrants for cash.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">DFDV believes the warrants provide the opportunity
to raise a meaningful amount of capital in a more cost-efficient manner than traditional equity offerings.&nbsp; The pricing reflects
our confidence in the company&rsquo;s growth trajectory and our commitment to raise capital in an efficient manner.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Can I sell my warrants? Will they trade
publicly?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The warrants are listed on the Nasdaq Capital
Market under ticker symbol DFDVW. DFDV stockholders, subject to the additional considerations outlined below, can trade or exercise the
warrants irrespective of whether they continue to hold or sell their shares of DFDV common stock.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Although the warrants have been registered
for trading under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, the issuance of the warrants was not registered under the Securities
Act of 1933, as amended, as the distribution of a warrant for no consideration does not constitute a sale of a security under Section
2(a)(3) of the Securities Act. Some stockholders may be subject to other securities law and company requirements that could restrict the
stockholder&rsquo;s ability to sell their warrants immediately. For example, company insiders are subject to compliance with the company&rsquo;s
insider trading policy. In addition, stockholders that hold shares that were issued by the company in transactions exempt from registration
under the Securities Act may not be able to sell or transfer their warrants if such sale or transfer does not meet the requirements of
Rule 144 under the Securities Act and in the absence of an effective registration statement for the resale of the warrants.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Can I receive a copy of the full warrant
agreement?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Yes. DFDV filed the full warrant agreement
with the SEC on the Form 8-A registration statement for the warrants, filed with the SEC on October 24, 2025. It is available via the
SEC&rsquo;s EDGAR system at www.sec.gov and linked on the DFDV Investor Relations page.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Will this dilute my ownership?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">There will be no dilution to DFDV stockholders
if no warrants are exercised. By the expiration date of January 21, 2028, we expect all warrants will have either expired or been exercised.
Since the warrants are being distributed pro-rata to all DFDV stockholders, if a stockholder decides to hold and exercise their warrants
to purchase additional shares their percentage ownership of DFDV common stock is not expected to be diluted. On the other hand, if a current
DFDV stockholder decides to sell their warrants in the market for cash, they will not be able to exercise and thus their percentage ownership
may decline.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>If warrants are exercised, what will DeFi
Development Corp. use the proceeds for?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">General corporate purposes, including the
acquisition of SOL and for working capital.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Will the company be receiving any proceeds
immediately?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">No. DeFi Development Corp. will not receive
any proceeds from this warrant distribution unless some or all holders exercise their warrants on or before the expiration date of January
21, 2028.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>What happens to my warrants if the share
price does not go up above the exercise price</B>?</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">If you do not sell or exercise your warrants
by the expiration date of January 21, 2028, or the early expiration date, if applicable, your warrants will expire. To be clear, you may
exercise a warrant at the exercise price even if the market price of DFDV shares does not go above the exercise price, but you may prefer
to instead purchase those shares in the market at a lower price.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>How does the Alternate Expiration Price
Condition work?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">If the Alternate Expiration Price Condition
is satisfied,&nbsp;the warrants will expire at 5:00 p.m. New York City time on the business day immediately following the Alternate Expiration
Price Condition Date (as defined below) or such other date as the Company may elect in accordance with the warrant agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">The Alternate Expiration
Price Condition will be deemed satisfied if, during any period of twenty (20) out of thirty (30) consecutive trading days, the VWAP of
the Company&rsquo;s common stock equals or exceeds $27.00 (the &ldquo;Alternate Expiration Trigger Price&rdquo;) whether or not consecutive
(such final day, the &ldquo;Alternate Expiration Price Condition Date&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">If the Alternate Expiration
Price Condition occurs, the Company will make a public announcement to that effect, which will include the corresponding expiration date.&nbsp;Otherwise,
as previously disclosed, the warrants will expire at 5:00 pm New York City Time on January 21, 2028.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>When does the 20 out of 30-day VWAP measurement
period for the Alternate Expiration Price Condition begin?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The 20 out of 30-day VWAP measurement period
can begin on the first trading day after the distribution date, as long as there is an effective shelf registration statement relating
to the issuance of the shares issuable on exercise of the warrants at such time.&nbsp; If Company shares are trading above $27.00 on that
day and the VWAP meets the threshold, that day counts as the first of the 20 qualifying days within the 30-trading-day window.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>If the VWAP Alternate Expiration Price
Condition is met, for example, on the 20th qualifying day, when do the warrants expire?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The warrants will expire on the business day
immediately following the 20th qualifying trading day within any 30-day period, unless the Company announces an alternate expiration date
in accordance with the warrant agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>How will I know if the warrants are about
to expire?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">If the warrants are scheduled to expire, either
on the final expiration date or due to early expiration, the Company will issue a public press release announcing the expiration date.
This notice will be made available as promptly as practicable and will include the exact date and time by which warrant exercises must
be completed.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">We encourage shareholders to monitor the Company&rsquo;s
Investor Relations website (https://defidevcorp.com/investor) for news announcements and updates, as well as our filings with the U.S.
Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;) at&nbsp;www.sec.gov.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>When can I exercise my warrants?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">You may exercise your warrants at any time
from the distribution date until the expiration date (or until any earlier deadline applied by your broker), subject to certain limited
exceptions included in the warrant agreement and assuming we have filed a registration statement, including a prospectus or prospectus
supplement relating to the exercise as described below on or before the distribution date, and that registration statement has become
effective.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>How do I exercise the warrants?</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">To exercise the warrants, you must have funds
available to pay the exercise price in cash. You should discuss with your broker its procedures and timeline for effecting exercise on
your behalf, because your broker may require you to give notice using a particular method and may require an earlier deadline than close
of business on the expiration date.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 3; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->3<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
